Hello,my name is Arthur. I come from P.R.China. 9 years ago, when I was still in college, I played postcrossing for a while. Now, I have settled down, started a family, and have a lovely daughter. Iâ€™m back!
(My avatar is my daughter who just turned one year old, her nickname is Xiaoxiao. Isnâ€™t she adorable?)If you want any ideas of postcards to send me, see below.
   *Xiaoxiao loves animals very much, any kind of cute animals postcards are welcome!
   *My wife is a clinical laboratory doctor and she also likes to watch TV series. Any postcards about doctors/local TV series recommendations are welcome.
   *I am very happy to receive postcards written in your language of your country.(e.g. greeting words for my family.)
   *series of the special festival of your country  
   *landscape from your own city / country 
   *Any other postcard you like
   By the way, I have recently developed a liking for coffee. Could you recommend any famous local coffee bean brands?   If you have sent me the postcard a long time ago and it hasnâ€™t been registered, you can let me know. My email is fsyflh@gmail.com. I will check my mailbox promptly.
  *It is recommended to print out the Chinese address and paste it on the postcard. It helped increase the delivery efficiency.

### æ”¶å‘è®°å½•ï¼ˆæœˆåº¦ï¼‰

:::echarts

```js
const data = await fetch(
  "https://raw.gitmirror.com/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator/main/output/month.json"
).then((res) => res.json());


var date = data.map(function (item) {
    return item.date
})

var sent = data.map(function (item) {
    return item.sent
})

var sentSum = sent.reduce(function(acc, curr) {
  return acc + curr;
}, 0);

var received = data.map(function (item) {
    return item.received
})

var receivedSum = received.reduce(function(acc, curr) {
  return acc + curr;
}, 0);

sentName = sentSum + "å¼ å·²å¯„å‡º"
receivedName = receivedSum + "å¼ å·²æ”¶åˆ°"

const option = {
  title: {
    text: '',
     left: 'center',
  },
    legend: {
    data: [sentName, receivedName]
  },
  tooltip: {
    trigger: 'axis'
  },
  xAxis: {
    type: 'category',
    data: date
  },
  yAxis: {
    type: 'value'
  },
  dataZoom: [
  {
    start: 0
  },
  {
    type: "inside"
  }
],
  series: [
    {
      name:sentName,
      data: sent,
      type: 'line',
      smooth: true
    },
    {
      name:receivedName,
      data: received,
      type: 'line',
      smooth: true
    }
  ]
}
```

:::

```js
const data = await fetch(
  "https://raw.gitmirror.com/arthurfsy2/Postcrossing_map_generator/main/output/stats.json"
).then((res) => res.json());

const option = {
  title: {
    text: "",
    subtext: "",
    left: "center"
  },
  tooltip: {
    trigger: 'item',
    formatter: '{a} <br/>{b} : {c} ({d}%)'
  },
  series: [
    {
      name: "",
      clockwise: false,
      type: "pie",
      radius: "50%",
      data: data,
      emphasis: {
        itemStyle: {
          shadowBlur: 10,
          shadowOffsetX: 0,
          shadowColor: "rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.5)"
        }
      },
      label: {
        alignTo: 'none',
        formatter: '{name|{b}}\n{num|{d}%}',
        minMargin: 1,
        fontStyle:'italic',
        fontWeight: 'bold',

        rich: {
          num: {
            fontSize: 10,
            color: '#999'
          }
        }
      },
      labelLine: {
        length: 50,

      }

    }
  ]
}
```

> Hello Siyuan, greetings from Leverkusen in the west of Germany! Today is the "1st day of Christmas", but in Germany the main day of celebrating Christmas is December 24th. Funnily, it's only the 25th and the 26th that are public holidays. But as this year the 24th fell on a Sunday, everyone had 3 days off. :) Frohes neues Jahr - Happy New Yeas! Hanna

> OSTRAVA!!
Lower Vitkovice is a national site of industrial heritage located in the Vitkovice district of Ostrava in the Czech Republic. it includes an extensive industrial area Vitkovice ironworks with a unique collection of industrial architecture. A set of threesuccessive parts - coal mine, coke ovens and blast fumnace operations - also called Ostrava Ostrava Hradcany, after Hradcanythe Castle District of Prague.
The area is registered in the list of European cultural heritage, and was placed on the Czech Republic's list of tentative UNESCO World Heritage Sites in 2001 under the name The Industrial Complexes at Ostrava.
Hi, I am Jitka from Ostrava, which is the third largest city in the Czech Republic. Have a nice day.
